# cs.CV [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [PathoScribe: Transforming Pathology Data into a Living Library with a Unified LLM-Driven Framework for Semantic Retrieval and Clinical Integration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08935)
*Abdul Rehman Akbar,Samuel Wales-McGrath,Alejadro Levya,Lina Gokhale,Rajendra Singh,Wei Chen,Anil Parwani,Muhammad Khalid Khan Niazi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: PathoScribe是一个基于检索增强大语言模型的统一框架，将静态病理档案转化为可搜索、支持推理的活体知识库，实现自然语言病例检索、自动队列构建、临床问答、免疫组化面板推荐和报告转换等功能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管病理学在现代诊断和癌症治疗中至关重要，但数百万份叙述性报告中积累的经验知识大多无法访问。机构正在数字化病理工作流程，但缺乏有效的检索和推理机制，导致档案成为被动数据仓库，无法有效指导临床决策。需要让病理学家在评估新诊断困境时能够实时查询类似病例。

Method: 开发了PathoScribe，一个统一的检索增强大语言模型框架。该系统支持自然语言病例探索、自动队列构建、临床问答、免疫组化面板推荐和提示控制报告转换。在70,000份多机构外科病理报告上进行了评估。

Result: PathoScribe在自然语言病例检索中实现了完美的Recall@10，检索增强推理获得平均4.56/5的评分。自动队列构建仅需平均9.2分钟，与人工评审一致性达91.3%，且无合格病例被错误排除，相比传统人工图表审查大幅减少时间和成本。

Conclusion: 这项工作为将数字病理档案从被动存储系统转化为主动临床智能平台建立了可扩展的基础，使机构知识能够有效指导患者护理。

Abstract: Pathology underpins modern diagnosis and cancer care, yet its most valuable asset, the accumulated experience encoded in millions of narrative reports, remains largely inaccessible. Although institutions are rapidly digitizing pathology workflows, storing data without effective mechanisms for retrieval and reasoning risks transforming archives into a passive data repository, where institutional knowledge exists but cannot meaningfully inform patient care. True progress requires not only digitization, but the ability for pathologists to interrogate prior similar cases in real time while evaluating a new diagnostic dilemma. We present PathoScribe, a unified retrieval-augmented large language model (LLM) framework designed to transform static pathology archives into a searchable, reasoning-enabled living library. PathoScribe enables natural language case exploration, automated cohort construction, clinical question answering, immunohistochemistry (IHC) panel recommendation, and prompt-controlled report transformation within a single architecture. Evaluated on 70,000 multi-institutional surgical pathology reports, PathoScribe achieved perfect Recall@10 for natural language case retrieval and demonstrated high-quality retrieval-grounded reasoning (mean reviewer score 4.56/5). Critically, the system operationalized automated cohort construction from free-text eligibility criteria, assembling research-ready cohorts in minutes (mean 9.2 minutes) with 91.3% agreement to human reviewers and no eligible cases incorrectly excluded, representing orders-of-magnitude reductions in time and cost compared to traditional manual chart review. This work establishes a scalable foundation for converting digital pathology archives from passive storage systems into active clinical intelligence platforms.

</details>


### [2] [Fine-grained Motion Retrieval via Joint-Angle Motion Images and Token-Patch Late Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09930)
*Yao Zhang,Zhuchenyang Liu,Yanlan He,Thomas Ploetz,Yu Xiao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种基于关节角度的可解释运动表示方法，通过伪图像映射和预训练视觉Transformer实现细粒度文本-运动检索，使用MaxSim机制和掩码语言建模正则化提升对齐效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文本-运动检索方法多采用双编码器框架，将运动和文本压缩为全局嵌入，丢弃了细粒度局部对应关系，降低了检索精度且缺乏结果可解释性。

Method: 提出基于关节角度的可解释运动表示，将关节级局部特征映射为结构化伪图像，兼容预训练视觉Transformer；使用MaxSim令牌级后期交互机制，并加入掩码语言建模正则化以增强鲁棒性和可解释性。

Result: 在HumanML3D和KIT-ML数据集上的实验表明，该方法在文本-运动检索任务上优于现有最先进方法，同时提供文本与运动之间可解释的细粒度对应关系。

Conclusion: 该方法通过细粒度、可解释的关节级表示和有效的跨模态对齐机制，显著提升了文本-运动检索的准确性和可解释性，为跨模态检索提供了新思路。

Abstract: Text-motion retrieval aims to learn a semantically aligned latent space between natural language descriptions and 3D human motion skeleton sequences, enabling bidirectional search across the two modalities. Most existing methods use a dual-encoder framework that compresses motion and text into global embeddings, discarding fine-grained local correspondences, and thus reducing accuracy. Additionally, these global-embedding methods offer limited interpretability of the retrieval results. To overcome these limitations, we propose an interpretable, joint-angle-based motion representation that maps joint-level local features into a structured pseudo-image, compatible with pre-trained Vision Transformers. For text-to-motion retrieval, we employ MaxSim, a token-wise late interaction mechanism, and enhance it with Masked Language Modeling regularization to foster robust, interpretable text-motion alignment. Extensive experiments on HumanML3D and KIT-ML show that our method outperforms state-of-the-art text-motion retrieval approaches while offering interpretable fine-grained correspondences between text and motion. The code is available in the supplementary material.

</details>


### [3] [A Lightweight Multi-Cancer Tumor Localization Framework for Deployable Digital Pathology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08844)
*Brian Isett,Rebekah Dadey,Aofei Li,Ryan C. Augustin,Kate Smith,Aatur D. Singhi,Qiangqiang Gu,Riyue Bao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: MuCTaL：一种多癌症肿瘤定位模型，通过平衡训练四种癌症类型，在验证数据上达到0.97 ROC-AUC，在未见胰腺癌数据上达到0.71 ROC-AUC，并构建了可扩展的推理工作流生成肿瘤概率热图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于深度学习的肿瘤检测模型在特定癌症类型上训练后，应用于不同肿瘤类型时可能表现出鲁棒性下降。研究旨在探索在适度规模下进行跨癌症平衡训练是否能够实现高性能并泛化到未见肿瘤类型。

Method: 使用DenseNet169进行迁移学习，在四种癌症（黑色素瘤、肝细胞癌、结直肠癌和非小细胞肺癌）的79,984个非重叠图像块上进行训练，构建多癌症肿瘤定位模型MuCTaL，并开发了可扩展的推理工作流生成空间肿瘤概率热图。

Result: 模型在四种训练癌症的验证数据上达到0.97的块级ROC-AUC，在独立的胰腺导管腺癌队列上达到0.71 ROC-AUC，表明模型具有良好的泛化能力。构建的工作流能够生成与现有数字病理工具兼容的空间肿瘤概率热图。

Conclusion: 平衡的跨癌症训练能够在适度规模下实现高性能的肿瘤定位，并具有一定的泛化能力到未见癌症类型。MuCTaL模型和代码已公开，为空间分析、分子谱分析和组织架构研究提供了实用工具。

Abstract: Accurate localization of tumor regions from hematoxylin and eosin-stained whole-slide images is fundamental for translational research including spatial analysis, molecular profiling, and tissue architecture investigation. However, deep learning-based tumor detection trained within specific cancers may exhibit reduced robustness when applied across different tumor types. We investigated whether balanced training across cancers at modest scale can achieve high performance and generalize to unseen tumor types. A multi-cancer tumor localization model (MuCTaL) was trained on 79,984 non-overlapping tiles from four cancers (melanoma, hepatocellular carcinoma, colorectal cancer, and non-small cell lung cancer) using transfer learning with DenseNet169. The model achieved a tile-level ROC-AUC of 0.97 in validation data from the four training cancers, and 0.71 on an independent pancreatic ductal adenocarcinoma cohort. A scalable inference workflow was built to generate spatial tumor probability heatmaps compatible with existing digital pathology tools. Code and models are publicly available at https://github.com/AivaraX-AI/MuCTaL.

</details>


### [4] [BiCLIP: Domain Canonicalization via Structured Geometric Transformation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08942)
*Pranav Mantini,Shishir K. Shah*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: BiCLIP：一种通过双线性变换增强跨模态对齐的极简框架，利用少量锚点估计域间几何变换，在11个基准测试中实现SOTA性能


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管视觉语言模型在零样本任务上表现出色，但适应专业领域仍具挑战性。基于理论发现——独立训练的VLMs可通过规范变换关联，本研究将此概念扩展到域层面，假设不同域的图像特征可通过规范化的几何变换关联，且该变换可通过少量锚点恢复

Method: 提出BiCLIP框架，对多模态特征应用目标变换以增强跨模态对齐。方法极其简单且参数量小，利用少样本分类中的有限标注样本作为锚点来估计域间变换

Result: 在包括EuroSAT、DTD、FGVCAircraft在内的11个标准基准测试上进行广泛评估，BiCLIP始终达到最先进的结果。通过分析学习变换的正交性和角度分布，为现有几何发现提供了实证验证

Conclusion: 结构化对齐是鲁棒域适应的关键。BiCLIP通过极简的双线性变换框架，利用少量锚点实现域间特征对齐，为视觉语言模型的领域适应提供了有效解决方案

Abstract: Recent advances in vision-language models (VLMs) have demonstrated remarkable zero-shot capabilities, yet adapting these models to specialized domains remains a significant challenge. Building on recent theoretical insights suggesting that independently trained VLMs are related by a canonical transformation, we extend this understanding to the concept of domains. We hypothesize that image features across disparate domains are related by a canonicalized geometric transformation that can be recovered using a small set of anchors. Few-shot classification provides a natural setting for this alignment, as the limited labeled samples serve as the anchors required to estimate this transformation. Motivated by this hypothesis, we introduce BiCLIP, a framework that applies a targeted transformation to multimodal features to enhance cross-modal alignment. Our approach is characterized by its extreme simplicity and low parameter footprint. Extensive evaluations across 11 standard benchmarks, including EuroSAT, DTD, and FGVCAircraft, demonstrate that BiCLIP consistently achieves state-of-the-art results. Furthermore, we provide empirical verification of existing geometric findings by analyzing the orthogonality and angular distribution of the learned transformations, confirming that structured alignment is the key to robust domain adaptation. Code is available at https://github.com/QuantitativeImagingLaboratory/BilinearCLIP

</details>


### [5] [WS-Net: Weak-Signal Representation Learning and Gated Abundance Reconstruction for Hyperspectral Unmixing via State-Space and Weak Signal Attention Fusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09037)
*Zekun Long,Ali Zia,Guanyiman Fu,Vivien Rolland,Jun Zhou*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: WS-Net：基于状态空间建模和弱信号注意力融合的深度解混框架，专门解决高光谱图像中弱光谱响应被主导端元和噪声掩盖的问题，显著提升弱端元丰度估计精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高光谱图像中的弱光谱响应常被主导端元和传感器噪声掩盖，导致丰度估计不准确。现有方法在处理弱信号时存在"弱信号崩溃"问题，需要专门设计框架来增强弱信号检测和分离能力。

Method: 提出WS-Net框架：1）多分辨率小波融合编码器捕捉高频不连续性和平滑光谱变化；2）混合主干集成Mamba状态空间分支用于高效长程依赖建模；3）弱信号注意力分支选择性增强低相似性光谱线索；4）可学习门控机制自适应融合两种表示；5）解码器利用KL散度正则化强制主导和弱端元之间的可分离性。

Result: 在一个模拟数据集和两个真实数据集（Samson和Apex）上的实验表明，相比六个最先进的基线方法，WS-Net在RMSE和SAD指标上分别实现了高达55%和63%的降低。该框架在低信噪比条件下保持稳定精度，特别是对弱端元，证明了其鲁棒性和计算效率。

Conclusion: WS-Net通过状态空间建模和弱信号注意力融合，有效解决了弱信号崩溃问题，成为弱信号高光谱解混的鲁棒且计算高效的基准框架，显著提升了弱端元的丰度估计精度。

Abstract: Weak spectral responses in hyperspectral images are often obscured by dominant endmembers and sensor noise, resulting in inaccurate abundance estimation. This paper introduces WS-Net, a deep unmixing framework specifically designed to address weak-signal collapse through state-space modelling and Weak Signal Attention fusion. The network features a multi-resolution wavelet-fused encoder that captures both high-frequency discontinuities and smooth spectral variations with a hybrid backbone that integrates a Mamba state-space branch for efficient long-range dependency modelling. It also incorporates a Weak Signal Attention branch that selectively enhances low-similarity spectral cues. A learnable gating mechanism adaptively fuses both representations, while the decoder leverages KL-divergence-based regularisation to enforce separability between dominant and weak endmembers. Experiments on one simulated and two real datasets (synthetic dataset, Samson, and Apex) demonstrate consistent improvements over six state-of-the-art baselines, achieving up to 55% and 63% reductions in RMSE and SAD, respectively. The framework maintains stable accuracy under low-SNR conditions, particularly for weak endmembers, establishing WS-Net as a robust and computationally efficient benchmark for weak-signal hyperspectral unmixing.

</details>


### [6] [GST-VLA: Structured Gaussian Spatial Tokens for 3D Depth-Aware Vision-Language-Action Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09079)
*Md Selim Sarowar,Omer Tariq,Sungho Kim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: GST-VLA：通过高斯空间标记器和3D深度感知思维链，将视觉语言模型与3D几何表示结合，提升机器人操作任务的性能


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统视觉语言模型（VLA）将视觉观测编码为无内在几何结构的2D补丁标记，缺乏对3D几何和空间关系的显式建模，限制了在需要精确几何推理的机器人操作任务中的性能

Method: 1. 高斯空间标记器（GST）：将冻结的密集深度和语义补丁特征转换为128个各向异性3D高斯基元，每个基元包含位置、协方差和对数不透明度参数；2. 3D深度感知思维链（DA-CoT）：监督四个结构化中间空间思维（3D物体定位、抓取接触几何、成对度量距离、粗SE(3)路径点）；3. 300M参数流匹配动作专家：通过条件ODE积分解码7自由度增量动作块，条件于VLM隐藏状态和DA-CoT输出

Result: 在LIBERO数据集上达到96.4%（提升2.0%），在SimplerEnv上达到80.2%（提升5.4%）。消融实验确认了每个GST组件、每个DA-CoT思维和每个训练阶段的独立和协同增益

Conclusion: GST-VLA通过显式的3D几何表示和结构化空间推理，显著提升了视觉语言模型在需要精确几何推理的机器人操作任务中的性能，特别是在精度要求高的任务上

Abstract: VLA models encode visual observations as 2D patch tokens with no intrinsic geometric structure. We introduce GST-VLA with two contributions. First, the Gaussian Spatial Tokenizer (GST) converts frozen dense depth and frozen semantic patch features into $N_g{=}128$ anisotropic 3D Gaussian primitives, each parameterized by a metric residual mean $μ\in \mathbb{R}^3$, log-scale covariance $\log σ\in \mathbb{R}^3$, and learned opacity $α\in (0,1)$. The covariance eigenstructure encodes local surface orientation, and opacity provides per-primitive geometric confidence, both inaccessible from scalar depth. Spatial attention pooling with learned queries concentrates the fixed token budget on geometrically salient regions rather than distributing uniformly. Second, 3D Depth-Aware Chain-of-Thought (DA-CoT) reasoning supervises four structured intermediate spatial thoughts, covering 3D object grounding, grasp affordance contact geometry, pairwise metric distances, and coarse SE(3) waypoints, as explicit generation targets in the training loss. A cross-attention sublayer at every VLM transformer block provides direct access to the raw 256-primitive Gaussian field during DA-CoT generation. A 300M-parameter flow-matching action expert with mixture-of-experts feedforward sublayers decodes 7-DoF delta action chunks via conditional ODE integration, conditioned on both VLM hidden states and DA-CoT outputs through dual cross-attention. Trained with composite $\mathcal{L}_\mathrm{flow} + \mathcal{L}_\mathrm{CoT} + \mathcal{L}_\mathrm{depth}$ across three progressive stages, GST-VLA achieves 96.4% on LIBERO (+2.0%), and 80.2% on SimplerEnv (+5.4%). Ablations isolate the contribution of each GST component, each DA-CoT thought, and each training stage, confirming independent and synergistic gains concentrated on precision demanding tasks.

</details>


### [7] [Composed Vision-Language Retrieval for Skin Cancer Case Search via Joint Alignment of Global and Local Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09108)
*Yuheng Wang,Yuji Lin,Dongrun Zhu,Jiayue Cai,Sunil Kalia,Harvey Lui,Chunqi Chang,Z. Jane Wang,Tim K. Lee*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出基于Transformer的层次化组合查询框架，用于皮肤癌的视觉-语言组合检索，通过全局-局部对齐和临床感知加权提升医学图像检索性能


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 医学图像检索在临床诊断、教育和质量控制中至关重要。实际查询通常结合病变图像和文本描述（如皮肤镜特征），需要有效处理这种组合查询来检索活检确认的多类疾病病例

Method: 提出基于Transformer的框架，学习层次化组合查询表示，执行查询与候选图像之间的联合全局-局部对齐。局部对齐通过多个空间注意力掩码聚合判别性区域，全局对齐提供整体语义监督。最终相似度通过凸的、领域感知的加权计算，强调临床显著的局部证据同时保持全局一致性

Result: 在公开的Derm7pt数据集上实验表明，相比最先进方法取得了一致的性能提升

Conclusion: 该框架能够高效访问相关医疗记录，支持实际临床部署，为皮肤癌诊断提供有效的组合检索解决方案

Abstract: Medical image retrieval aims to identify clinically relevant lesion cases to support diagnostic decision making, education, and quality control. In practice, retrieval queries often combine a reference lesion image with textual descriptors such as dermoscopic features. We study composed vision-language retrieval for skin cancer, where each query consists of an image to text pair and the database contains biopsy-confirmed, multi-class disease cases. We propose a transformer based framework that learns hierarchical composed query representations and performs joint global-local alignment between queries and candidate images. Local alignment aggregates discriminative regions via multiple spatial attention masks, while global alignment provides holistic semantic supervision. The final similarity is computed through a convex, domain-informed weighting that emphasizes clinically salient local evidence while preserving global consistency. Experiments on the public Derm7pt dataset demonstrate consistent improvements over state-of-the-art methods. The proposed framework enables efficient access to relevant medical records and supports practical clinical deployment.

</details>


### [8] [QUSR: Quality-Aware and Uncertainty-Guided Image Super-Resolution Diffusion Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09125)
*Junjie Yin,Jiaju Li,Hanfa Xing*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: QUSR：一种结合质量感知先验和不确定性引导噪声生成的扩散超分辨率模型，用于处理真实世界中的未知和非均匀退化问题


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于扩散的图像超分辨率方法在真实场景中面临挑战，因为退化通常是未知且空间非均匀的，导致细节丢失或视觉伪影。需要一种能够自适应处理不同区域不确定性并利用质量先验的方法。

Method: 提出QUSR模型，包含两个核心组件：1）不确定性引导噪声生成（UNG）模块，根据区域不确定性自适应调整噪声注入强度，对高不确定性区域（如边缘和纹理）施加更强扰动以重建复杂细节，对低不确定性区域（如平坦区域）最小化噪声以保留原始信息；2）质量感知先验（QAP），利用先进的多模态大语言模型生成可靠的质量描述，为恢复过程提供有效且可解释的质量先验。

Result: 实验结果表明，QUSR能够在真实世界场景中生成高保真度和高真实感的图像。模型源代码已公开。

Conclusion: QUSR通过结合不确定性引导的噪声生成和质量感知先验，有效解决了真实世界超分辨率中的未知和非均匀退化问题，实现了更好的细节重建和视觉质量。

Abstract: Diffusion-based image super-resolution (ISR) has shown strong potential, but it still struggles in real-world scenarios where degradations are unknown and spatially non-uniform, often resulting in lost details or visual artifacts. To address this challenge, we propose a novel super-resolution diffusion model, QUSR, which integrates a Quality-Aware Prior (QAP) with an Uncertainty-Guided Noise Generation (UNG) module. The UNG module adaptively adjusts the noise injection intensity, applying stronger perturbations to high-uncertainty regions (e.g., edges and textures) to reconstruct complex details, while minimizing noise in low-uncertainty regions (e.g., flat areas) to preserve original information. Concurrently, the QAP leverages an advanced Multimodal Large Language Model (MLLM) to generate reliable quality descriptions, providing an effective and interpretable quality prior for the restoration process. Experimental results confirm that QUSR can produce high-fidelity and high-realism images in real-world scenarios. The source code is available at https://github.com/oTvTog/QUSR.

</details>


### [9] [RubiCap: Rubric-Guided Reinforcement Learning for Dense Image Captioning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09160)
*Tzu-Heng Huang,Sirajul Salekin,Javier Movellan,Frederic Sala,Manjot Bilkhu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: RubiCap是一个新颖的强化学习框架，通过LLM编写的评估准则为密集图像描述生成提供细粒度、样本特定的奖励信号，解决了传统监督蒸馏输出多样性有限和弱泛化的问题，在多个基准测试中表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 密集图像描述在视觉-语言预训练和文本到图像生成中至关重要，但专家级标注成本高昂。虽然通过强视觉语言模型进行合成描述是实用替代方案，但监督蒸馏通常输出多样性有限且泛化能力弱。强化学习可以克服这些限制，但以往成功主要集中在依赖确定性检查器的可验证领域，而开放式的图像描述缺乏这种条件。

Method: RubiCap框架首先组建候选描述的多样化委员会，然后使用LLM准则编写器提取共识优势并诊断当前策略的缺陷。这些见解被转化为明确的评估标准，使LLM评判器能够分解整体质量评估，用结构化的多维度评估替代粗糙的标量奖励。

Conclusion: RubiCap通过LLM编写的准则为密集图像描述强化学习提供细粒度奖励信号，有效解决了传统方法的局限性，在多个指标上超越了现有方法，包括监督蒸馏、先前RL方法和人类专家标注，展示了在视觉-语言任务中的显著优势。

Abstract: Dense image captioning is critical for cross-modal alignment in vision-language pretraining and text-to-image generation, but scaling expert-quality annotations is prohibitively expensive. While synthetic captioning via strong vision-language models (VLMs) is a practical alternative, supervised distillation often yields limited output diversity and weak generalization. Reinforcement learning (RL) could overcome these limitations, but its successes have so far been concentrated in verifiable domains that rely on deterministic checkers -- a luxury not available in open-ended captioning. We address this bottleneck with RubiCap, a novel RL framework that derives fine-grained, sample-specific reward signals from LLM-written rubrics. RubiCap first assembles a diverse committee of candidate captions, then employs an LLM rubric writer to extract consensus strengths and diagnose deficiencies in the current policy. These insights are converted into explicit evaluation criteria, enabling an LLM judge to decompose holistic quality assessment and replace coarse scalar rewards with structured, multi-faceted evaluations. Across extensive benchmarks, RubiCap achieves the highest win rates on CapArena, outperforming supervised distillation, prior RL methods, human-expert annotations, and GPT-4V-augmented outputs. On CaptionQA, it demonstrates superior word efficiency: our 7B model matches Qwen2.5-VL-32B-Instruct, and our 3B model surpasses its 7B counterpart. We propose BridgeDiff, a diffusion-based framework that explicitly bridges human-centric observations and flat-garment synthesis through two complementary components. Second, the Flat Structure Constraint Module (FSCM) injects explicit flat-garment structural priors via Flat-Constraint Attention (FC-Attention) at selected denoising stages, improving structural stability beyond text-only conditioning. We present \textbf{SpaceSense-Bench}, a large-scale multi-modal benchmark for spacecraft perception encompassing 136~satellite models with approximately 70~GB of data. Each frame provides time-synchronized 1024$\times$1024 RGB images, millimeter-precision depth maps, and 256-beam LiDAR point clouds, together with dense 7-class part-level semantic labels at both the pixel and point level as well as accurate 6-DoF pose ground truth. The dataset is generated through a high-fidelity space simulation built in Unreal Engine~5 and a fully automated pipeline covering data acquisition, multi-stage quality control, and conversion to mainstream formats. We benchmark five representative tasks (object detection, 2D semantic segmentation, RGB--LiDAR fusion-based 3D point cloud segmentation, monocular depth estimation, and orientation estimation) and identify two key findings: (i)~perceiving small-scale components (\emph{e.g.}, thrusters and omni-antennas) and generalizing to entirely unseen spacecraft in a zero-shot setting remain critical bottlenecks for current methods, and (ii)~scaling up the number of training satellites yields substantial performance gains on novel targets, underscoring the value of large-scale, diverse datasets for space perception research. Result: 广泛配对评估显示明显的策略-执行差距：推理密集型模型在回合制设置中占优，但推理延迟导致在实时场景中表现较差，而更快的指令调优模型在实时环境中表现更好。

This paper introduces Strategic Tactical Agent Reasoning (STAR) Benchmark, a multi-agent evaluation framework that assesses LLMs through 1v1 zero-sum competitive interactions, framing reasoning as an iterative, adaptive decision-making process. STAR supports both turn-based and real-time settings, enabling controlled analysis of long-horizon strategic planning and fast-paced tactical execution within a unified environment. Built on a modular architecture with a standardized API and fully implemented execution engine, STAR facilitates reproducible evaluation and flexible task customization. To move beyond binary win-loss outcomes, we introduce a Strategic Evaluation Suite that assesses not only competitive success but also the quality of strategic behavior, such as execution efficiency and outcome stability. Extensive pairwise evaluations reveal a pronounced strategy-execution gap: while reasoning-intensive models dominate turn-based settings, their inference latency often leads to inferior performance in real-time scenarios, where faster instruction-tuned models prevail. These results show that strategic intelligence in interactive environments depends not only on reasoning depth, but also on the ability to translate plans into timely actions, positioning STAR as a principled benchmark for studying this trade-off in competitive, dynamic settings.

### [13] [M3GCLR: Multi-View Mini-Max Infinite Skeleton-Data Game Contrastive Learning For Skeleton-Based Action Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09367)
*Yanshan Li,Ke Ma,Miaomiao Wei,Linhui Dai*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出M3GCLR框架，通过博弈论对比学习解决骨架动作识别中视图差异建模不足、对抗机制缺乏和增强扰动不可控三大问题，在多数据集上达到SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自监督骨架动作识别方法存在三个主要限制：1) 视图差异建模不足；2) 缺乏有效对抗机制；3) 增强扰动不可控。这些问题限制了模型从无标签数据中学习判别性特征的能力。

Method: 提出M3GCLR框架：1) 建立无限骨架数据博弈模型及均衡定理；2) 通过多视图旋转增强生成正常-极端数据对，使用时序平均输入作为中性锚点实现结构对齐；3) 构建强对抗性极小极大骨架数据博弈；4) 引入双损失均衡优化器优化博弈均衡。

Result: 在NTU RGB+D 60数据集上达到三流82.1%(X-Sub)和85.8%(X-View)准确率；在NTU RGB+D 120上达到72.3%(X-Sub)和75.0%(X-Set)；在PKU-MMD Part I和II上分别达到89.1%和45.2%，均匹配或超越SOTA性能。

Conclusion: M3GCLR通过博弈论对比学习框架有效解决了现有方法的三大限制，在多视图建模、对抗机制和扰动控制方面取得显著改进，为自监督骨架动作识别提供了新的理论框架和实践方案。

Abstract: In recent years, contrastive learning has drawn significant attention as an effective approach to reducing reliance on labeled data. However, existing methods for self-supervised skeleton-based action recognition still face three major limitations: insufficient modeling of view discrepancies, lack of effective adversarial mechanisms, and uncontrollable augmentation perturbations. To tackle these issues, we propose the Multi-view Mini-Max infinite skeleton-data Game Contrastive Learning for skeleton-based action Recognition (M3GCLR), a game-theoretic contrastive framework. First, we establish the Infinite Skeleton-data Game (ISG) model and the ISG equilibrium theorem, and further provide a rigorous proof, enabling mini-max optimization based on multi-view mutual information. Then, we generate normal-extreme data pairs through multi-view rotation augmentation and adopt temporally averaged input as a neutral anchor to achieve structural alignment, thereby explicitly characterizing perturbation strength. Next, leveraging the proposed equilibrium theorem, we construct a strongly adversarial mini-max skeleton-data game to encourage the model to mine richer action-discriminative information. Finally, we introduce the dual-loss equilibrium optimizer to optimize the game equilibrium, allowing the learning process to maximize action-relevant information while minimizing encoding redundancy, and we prove the equivalence between the proposed optimizer and the ISG model. Extensive Experiments show that M3GCLR achieves three-stream 82.1%, 85.8% accuracy on NTU RGB+D 60 (X-Sub, X-View) and 72.3%, 75.0% accuracy on NTU RGB+D 120 (X-Sub, X-Set). On PKU-MMD Part I and II, it attains 89.1%, 45.2% in three-stream respectively, all results matching or outperforming state-of-the-art performance. Ablation studies confirm the effectiveness of each component.

### [16] [Open-World Motion Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09420)
*Nicolas Schischka,Nikhil Gosala,B Ravi Kiran,Senthil Yogamani,Abhinav Valada*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出首个端到端类增量运动预测框架，解决自动驾驶中感知不完美和对象分类随时间演变的问题，通过伪标签策略和重放采样缓解灾难性遗忘。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有运动预测方法在封闭世界假设下工作，依赖高质量感知和固定对象分类，难以适应现实世界中感知不完美和对象分类随时间演变的情况。需要开发能够处理新对象类别逐步引入的开放世界运动预测方法。

Method: 提出首个端到端类增量运动预测框架：1) 使用伪标签策略为新类别生成运动预测标签；2) 利用视觉语言模型过滤不一致和过度自信的预测；3) 采用基于查询特征方差的重放采样策略，选择具有信息性运动模式的先前序列来缓解灾难性遗忘。

Result: 在nuScenes和Argoverse 2数据集上的广泛评估表明，该方法成功抵抗灾难性遗忘，保持对已学习类别的性能，同时提高对新类别的适应能力。支持零样本迁移到真实世界驾驶，并可扩展到端到端类增量规划。

Conclusion: 该工作首次提出开放世界运动预测设置和相应的类增量学习框架，解决了自动驾驶系统中感知不完美和对象分类演变的现实挑战，为完整的自动驾驶系统持续适应提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Motion forecasting aims to predict the future trajectories of dynamic agents in the scene, enabling autonomous vehicles to effectively reason about scene evolution. Existing approaches operate under the closed-world regime and assume fixed object taxonomy as well as access to high-quality perception. Therefore, they struggle in real-world settings where perception is imperfect and object taxonomy evolves over time. In this work, we bridge this fundamental gap by introducing open-world motion forecasting, a novel setting in which new object classes are sequentially introduced over time and future object trajectories are estimated directly from camera images. We tackle this setting by proposing the first end-to-end class-incremental motion forecasting framework to mitigate catastrophic forgetting while simultaneously learning to forecast newly introduced classes. When a new class is introduced, our framework employs a pseudo-labeling strategy to first generate motion forecasting pseudo-labels for all known classes which are then processed by a vision-language model to filter inconsistent and over-confident predictions. Parallelly, our approach further mitigates catastrophic forgetting by using a novel replay sampling strategy that leverages query feature variance to sample previous sequences with informative motion patterns. Extensive evaluation on the nuScenes and Argoverse 2 datasets demonstrates that our approach successfully resists catastrophic forgetting and maintains performance on previously learned classes while improving adaptation to novel ones. Further, we demonstrate that our approach supports zero-shot transfer to real-world driving and naturally extends to end-to-end class-incremental planning, enabling continual adaptation of the full autonomous driving system. We provide the code at https://omen.cs.uni-freiburg.de .

</details>


### [17] [EvoDriveVLA: Evolving Autonomous Driving Vision-Language-Action Model via Collaborative Perception-Planning Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09465)
*Jiajun Cao,Xiaoan Zhang,Xiaobao Wei,Liyuqiu Huang,Wang Zijian,Hanzhen Zhang,Zhengyu Jia,Wei Mao,Hao Wang,Xianming Liu,Shuchang Zhou Liu,Yang Wang,Shanghang Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: EvoDriveVLA提出了一种协作感知-规划蒸馏框架，通过自锚定视觉蒸馏和先知引导轨迹蒸馏解决VLA模型在自动驾驶中的感知退化和长期规划不稳定问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前视觉-语言-动作模型在自动驾驶中存在两个主要问题：1) 解冻视觉编码器后感知性能下降；2) 长期规划中累积的不稳定性。这些问题限制了VLA模型在实际自动驾驶场景中的可靠性和性能。

Method: 提出协作感知-规划蒸馏框架EvoDriveVLA，包含两个核心组件：1) 自锚定视觉蒸馏：利用自锚定教师模型提供视觉锚定约束，通过轨迹引导的关键区域感知来正则化学生模型表示；2) 先知引导轨迹蒸馏：使用未来感知的先知教师模型，结合粗到细的轨迹优化和蒙特卡洛dropout采样，生成高质量轨迹候选，选择最优轨迹指导学生模型预测。

Result: EvoDriveVLA在开环评估中达到了最先进的性能，同时在闭环评估中显著提升了性能表现。

Conclusion: EvoDriveVLA通过创新的协作感知-规划蒸馏框架，有效解决了VLA模型在自动驾驶中的感知退化和规划不稳定问题，为自动驾驶系统提供了更可靠和高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action models have shown great promise for autonomous driving, yet they suffer from degraded perception after unfreezing the visual encoder and struggle with accumulated instability in long-term planning. To address these challenges, we propose EvoDriveVLA-a novel collaborative perception-planning distillation framework that integrates self-anchored perceptual constraints and oracle-guided trajectory optimization. Specifically, self-anchored visual distillation leverages self-anchor teacher to deliver visual anchoring constraints, regularizing student representations via trajectory-guided key-region awareness. In parallel, oracle-guided trajectory distillation employs a future-aware oracle teacher with coarse-to-fine trajectory refinement and Monte Carlo dropout sampling to produce high-quality trajectory candidates, thereby selecting the optimal trajectory to guide the student's prediction. EvoDriveVLA achieves SOTA performance in open-loop evaluation and significantly enhances performance in closed-loop evaluation. Our code is available at: https://github.com/hey-cjj/EvoDriveVLA.

### [18] [Evolving Prompt Adaptation for Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09493)
*Enming Zhang,Jiayang Li,Yanru Wu,Zhenyu Liu,Yang Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: EvoPrompt是一个新颖的提示学习框架，通过显式控制提示演化轨迹来解决视觉语言模型在少样本下游任务适应中的灾难性遗忘问题，实现知识保留的稳定微调。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模视觉语言模型在有限标注数据的下游任务适应中存在灾难性遗忘预训练知识的问题，现有参数高效的提示学习方法难以平衡新任务学习和知识保留。

Method: 提出EvoPrompt框架：1）使用模态共享提示投影器从统一嵌入空间生成分层提示；2）演化训练策略将低秩更新解耦为方向和幅度分量，保留早期学习的语义方向仅调整幅度；3）特征几何正则化强制特征去相关防止表示崩溃。

Result: 在少样本学习任务中达到最先进性能，同时鲁棒地保持预训练视觉语言模型的原始零样本能力，有效解决了灾难性遗忘问题。

Conclusion: 通过显式控制提示演化轨迹，EvoPrompt实现了稳定、知识保留的视觉语言模型适应，为参数高效的少样本学习提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: The adaptation of large-scale vision-language models (VLMs) to downstream tasks with limited labeled data remains a significant challenge. While parameter-efficient prompt learning methods offer a promising path, they often suffer from catastrophic forgetting of pre-trained knowledge. Toward addressing this limitation, our work is grounded in the insight that governing the evolutionary path of prompts is essential for forgetting-free adaptation. To this end, we propose EvoPrompt, a novel framework designed to explicitly steer the prompt trajectory for stable, knowledge-preserving fine-tuning. Specifically, our approach employs a Modality-Shared Prompt Projector (MPP) to generate hierarchical prompts from a unified embedding space. Critically, an evolutionary training strategy decouples low-rank updates into directional and magnitude components, preserving early-learned semantic directions while only adapting their magnitude, thus enabling prompts to evolve without discarding foundational knowledge. This process is further stabilized by Feature Geometric Regularization (FGR), which enforces feature decorrelation to prevent representation collapse. Extensive experiments demonstrate that EvoPrompt achieves state-of-the-art performance in few-shot learning while robustly preserving the original zero-shot capabilities of pre-trained VLMs.

Abstract: Deep learning models benefit from increasing data diversity and volume, motivating synthetic data augmentation to improve existing datasets.   We propose a vision-language grounded framework for interpretable synthetic data augmentation and evaluation in remote sensing. Our approach combines generative models, semantic segmentation and image captioning with vision and language models. Based on this framework, we introduce ARAS400k: A large-scale Remote sensing dataset Augmented with Synthetic data for segmentation and captioning, containing 100k real images and 300k synthetic images, each paired with segmentation maps and descriptions.
  ARAS400k enables the automated evaluation of synthetic data by analyzing semantic composition, minimizing caption redundancy, and verifying cross-modal consistency between visual structures and language descriptions. Experimental results indicate that while models trained exclusively on synthetic data reach competitive performance levels, those trained with augmented data (a combination of real and synthetic images) consistently outperform real-data baselines. Consequently, this work establishes a scalable benchmark for remote sensing tasks, specifically in semantic segmentation and image captioning. The dataset is available at zenodo.org/records/18890661 and the code base at github.com/caglarmert/ARAS400k.

### [20] [When to Lock Attention: Training-Free KV Control in Video Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09657)
*Tianyi Zeng,Jincheng Gao,Tianyi Wang,Zijie Meng,Miao Zhang,Jun Yin,Haoyuan Sun,Junfeng Jiao,Christian Claudel,Junbo Tan,Xueqian Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: KV-Lock：基于DiT的视频扩散模型训练免费框架，通过动态调度背景KV缓存融合比和CFG尺度，在保持背景一致性的同时提升前景生成质量


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视频编辑中保持背景一致性同时提升前景质量是核心挑战。注入全图信息会导致背景伪影，而严格的背景锁定又严重限制了模型的前景生成能力。需要一种平衡方法来同时保证背景保真度和前景质量。

Method: 提出KV-Lock训练免费框架，核心洞察是幻觉指标（去噪预测方差）直接量化生成多样性，与CFG尺度内在相关。利用扩散幻觉检测动态调度两个关键组件：缓存背景KV与新生成KV的融合比，以及CFG尺度。当检测到幻觉风险时，加强背景KV锁定并同时增强条件引导，从而减轻伪影并提高生成保真度。

Result: 作为训练免费、即插即用模块，KV-Lock可轻松集成到任何预训练的DiT模型中。大量实验验证该方法在各种视频编辑任务中，在保持高背景保真度的同时，提升了前景质量，优于现有方法。

Conclusion: KV-Lock通过动态调度背景KV融合和CFG尺度，有效解决了视频编辑中背景一致性与前景质量的平衡问题，为DiT基视频扩散模型提供了实用的训练免费解决方案。

Abstract: Maintaining background consistency while enhancing foreground quality remains a core challenge in video editing. Injecting full-image information often leads to background artifacts, whereas rigid background locking severely constrains the model's capacity for foreground generation. To address this issue, we propose KV-Lock, a training-free framework tailored for DiT-based video diffusion models. Our core insight is that the hallucination metric (variance of denoising prediction) directly quantifies generation diversity, which is inherently linked to the classifier-free guidance (CFG) scale. Building upon this, KV-Lock leverages diffusion hallucination detection to dynamically schedule two key components: the fusion ratio between cached background key-values (KVs) and newly generated KVs, and the CFG scale. When hallucination risk is detected, KV-Lock strengthens background KV locking and simultaneously amplifies conditional guidance for foreground generation, thereby mitigating artifacts and improving generation fidelity. As a training-free, plug-and-play module, KV-Lock can be easily integrated into any pre-trained DiT-based models. Extensive experiments validate that our method outperforms existing approaches in improved foreground quality with high background fidelity across various video editing tasks.

Method: 提出新任务"自我中心场景预测与长时序推理"：给定初始场景图像和原子动作序列，预测执行所有动作后的最终场景。构建EXPLORE-Bench基准，从真实第一人称视频中提取数据，包含长动作序列和结构化最终场景标注（对象类别、视觉属性、对象间关系）。

To enable systematic evaluation, we introduce EXPLORE-Bench, a benchmark curated from real first-person videos spanning diverse scenarios. Each instance pairs long action sequences with structured final-scene annotations, including object categories, visual attributes, and inter-object relations, which supports fine-grained, quantitative assessment. Experiments on a range of proprietary and open-source MLLMs reveal a significant performance gap to humans, indicating that long-horizon egocentric reasoning remains a major challenge. We further analyze test-time scaling via stepwise reasoning and show that decomposing long action sequences can improve performance to some extent, while incurring non-trivial computational overhead. Overall, EXPLORE-Bench provides a principled testbed for measuring and advancing long-horizon reasoning for egocentric embodied perception.

Existing challenges include effectively compressing and communicating high volumes of individual sensory inputs in the form of video and correctly aggregating multiple egocentric videos to construct system-level memory. In this work, we first formally define a novel problem of understanding multiple long-horizon egocentric videos simultaneously collected from embodied agents. MA-EgoQA provides 1.7k questions unique to multiple egocentric streams, spanning five categories: social interaction, task coordination, theory-of-mind, temporal reasoning, and environmental interaction. Through comprehensive evaluation across diverse baselines and EgoMAS on MA-EgoQA, we find that current approaches are unable to effectively handle multiple egocentric streams, highlighting the need for future advances in system-level understanding across the agents. ### [25] [Adaptive Clinical-Aware Latent Diffusion for Multimodal Brain Image Generation and Missing Modality Imputation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09931)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在ADNI受试者上评估，ACADiff实现了卓越的生成质量，在极端80%缺失情况下仍保持稳健的诊断性能，优于所有现有基线方法。

Conclusion: ACADiff能够有效合成缺失的多模态脑成像数据，提升阿尔茨海默病诊断的鲁棒性，特别是在临床数据不完整的情况下具有重要应用价值。

Abstract: Multimodal neuroimaging provides complementary insights for Alzheimer's disease diagnosis, yet clinical datasets frequently suffer from missing modalities. We propose ACADiff, a framework that synthesizes missing brain imaging modalities through adaptive clinical-aware diffusion. ACADiff learns mappings between incomplete multimodal observations and target modalities by progressively denoising latent representations while attending to available imaging data and clinical metadata. The framework employs adaptive fusion that dynamically reconfigures based on input availability, coupled with semantic clinical guidance via GPT-4o-encoded prompts. Three specialized generators enable bidirectional synthesis among sMRI, FDG-PET, and AV45-PET. Evaluated on ADNI subjects, ACADiff achieves superior generation quality and maintains robust diagnostic performance even under extreme 80\% missing scenarios, outperforming all existing baselines. To promote reproducibility, code is available at https://github.com/rongzhou7/ACADiff

</details>


### [26] [No Image, No Problem: End-to-End Multi-Task Cardiac Analysis from Undersampled k-Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09945)
*Yundi Zhang,Sevgi Gokce Kafali,Niklas Bubeck,Daniel Rueckert,Jiazhen Pan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: k-MTR是一种直接从欠采样k空间学习多任务表示的框架，绕过传统的"重建-分析"流程，将欠采样k空间与全采样图像对齐到共享语义流形中，实现直接从k空间提取诊断特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统心脏磁共振(CMR)流程采用"重建-分析"的串行范式，需要从欠采样k空间恢复完整图像，这是一个病态逆问题，会引入伪影和信息瓶颈。实际上诊断只需要低维生理标签，而非高维像素阵列，因此需要直接从k空间提取诊断信息。

Method: 提出k-MTR框架，将欠采样k空间数据和全采样图像对齐到共享语义流形中。利用42,000个受试者的大规模模拟数据，强制k空间编码器在潜在空间中恢复因欠采样丢失的解剖信息，绕过显式逆问题。通过潜在对齐，从欠采样频率直接嵌入高级生理语义的密集潜在空间。

Result: 在连续表型回归、疾病分类和解剖分割任务中，k-MTR实现了与最先进图像域基线方法相竞争的性能。证明可以从k空间表示中成功恢复精确的空间几何结构和多任务特征。

Conclusion: k-MTR为任务感知的心脏MRI工作流程提供了稳健的架构蓝图，展示了直接从k空间表示中提取诊断信息的可行性，突破了传统重建-分析范式的局限性。

Abstract: Conventional clinical CMR pipelines rely on a sequential "reconstruct-then-analyze" paradigm, forcing an ill-posed intermediate step that introduces avoidable artifacts and information bottlenecks. This creates a fundamental mathematical paradox: it attempts to recover high-dimensional pixel arrays (i.e., images) from undersampled k-space, rather than directly extracting the low-dimensional physiological labels actually required for diagnosis. To unlock the direct diagnostic potential of k-space, we propose k-MTR (k-space Multi-Task Representation), a k-space representation learning framework that aligns undersampled k-space data and fully-sampled images into a shared semantic manifold. Leveraging a large-scale controlled simulation of 42,000 subjects, k-MTR forces the k-space encoder to restore anatomical information lost to undersampling directly within the latent space, bypassing the explicit inverse problem for downstream analysis. We demonstrate that this latent alignment enables the dense latent space embedded with high-level physiological semantics directly from undersampled frequencies. Across continuous phenotype regression, disease classification, and anatomical segmentation, k-MTR achieves highly competitive performance against state-of-the-art image-domain baselines. By showcasing that precise spatial geometries and multi-task features can be successfully recovered directly from the k-space representations, k-MTR provides a robust architectural blueprint for task-aware cardiac MRI workflows.

</details>

### [27] [Understanding the Interplay between LLMs' Utilisation of Parametric and Contextual Knowledge: A keynote at ECIR 2025](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09654)
*Isabelle Augenstein*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文探讨语言模型参数知识与上下文知识之间的冲突问题，提出评估方法、诊断测试和理解成功使用上下文知识的特征


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着语言模型规模扩大，理解其内部工作机制和更新嵌入知识变得困难且成本高昂。模型在处理知识密集型任务时需要整合上下文，但常常忽略与预训练记忆冲突的上下文信息，存在参数内部的知识冲突问题

Method: 提出评估语言模型中知识存在的方法，开发诊断测试以揭示知识冲突，并分析成功使用上下文知识的特征

Result: 揭示了语言模型参数知识与上下文知识之间的复杂相互作用，提供了诊断知识冲突的工具，并识别了成功整合上下文知识的关键特征

Conclusion: 理解语言模型如何使用参数知识和检索的上下文知识之间的相互作用至关重要，该研究为解决知识冲突问题提供了评估框架和分析工具

Abstract: Language Models (LMs) acquire parametric knowledge from their training process, embedding it within their weights. The increasing scalability of LMs, however, poses significant challenges for understanding a model's inner workings and further for updating or correcting this embedded knowledge without the significant cost of retraining. Moreover, when using these language models for knowledge-intensive language understanding tasks, LMs have to integrate relevant context, mitigating their inherent weaknesses, such as incomplete or outdated knowledge. Nevertheless, studies indicate that LMs often ignore the provided context as it can be in conflict with the pre-existing LM's memory learned during pre-training. Conflicting knowledge can also already be present in the LM's parameters, termed intra-memory conflict. This underscores the importance of understanding the interplay between how a language model uses its parametric knowledge and the retrieved contextual knowledge. In this talk, I will aim to shed light on this important issue by presenting our research on evaluating the knowledge present in LMs, diagnostic tests that can reveal knowledge conflicts, as well as on understanding the characteristics of successfully used contextual knowledge.

</details>


### [28] [Automatic Cardiac Risk Management Classification using large-context Electronic Patients Health Records](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09685)
*Jacopo Vitale,David Della Morte,Luca Bacco,Mario Merone,Mark de Groot,Saskia Haitjema,Leandro Pecchia,Bram van Es*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 开发自动化分类框架，利用非结构化电子健康记录进行老年心血管风险管理，比较三种建模范式，发现定制Transformer架构在性能上优于传统方法和生成式大语言模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 克服老年心血管风险管理中手动管理编码的局限性，为临床风险分层提供自动化替代方案。

Method: 使用3,482名患者数据集，在荷兰纵向临床叙述上基准测试三种建模范式：经典机器学习基线、针对大上下文序列优化的专业深度学习架构、零样本设置下的通用生成式大语言模型，并评估了将非结构化文本与结构化药物嵌入和人体测量数据整合的后期融合策略。

Result: 定制Transformer架构在F1分数和Matthews相关系数方面均优于传统方法和生成式大语言模型，表现出最佳性能。

Conclusion: 专业的分层注意力机制在捕捉医学文本中的长距离依赖关系方面发挥关键作用，为临床风险分层提供了稳健的自动化替代方案。

Abstract: To overcome the limitations of manual administrative coding in geriatric Cardiovascular Risk Management, this study introduces an automated classification framework leveraging unstructured Electronic Health Records (EHRs). Using a dataset of 3,482 patients, we benchmarked three distinct modeling paradigms on longitudinal Dutch clinical narratives: classical machine learning baselines, specialized deep learning architectures optimized for large-context sequences, and general-purpose generative Large Language Models (LLMs) in a zero-shot setting. Additionally, we evaluated a late fusion strategy to integrate unstructured text with structured medication embeddings and anthropometric data. Our analysis reveals that the custom Transformer architecture outperforms both traditional methods and generative \acs{llm}s, achieving the highest F1-scores and Matthews Correlation Coefficients. These findings underscore the critical role of specialized hierarchical attention mechanisms in capturing long-range dependencies within medical texts, presenting a robust, automated alternative to manual workflows for clinical risk stratification.

### [29] [Let's Verify Math Questions Step by Step](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.13903)
*Chengyu Shen,Zhen Hao Wong,Runming He,Hao Liang,Meiyi Qiang,Zimo Meng,Zhengyang Zhao,Bohan Zeng,Zhengzhou Zhu,Bin Cui,Wentao Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MathQ-Verify：一个五阶段验证管道，用于过滤数学问题中的病态或欠规范问题，提高数学数据集质量


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要关注生成正确的推理路径和答案，但忽视了问题本身的有效性。许多数学问题存在病态或欠规范的情况，这会影响数据集质量和模型训练效果。

Method: 提出MathQ-Verify五阶段验证管道：1) 格式级验证，去除冗余指令并确保语法正确；2) 问题形式化，分解为原子条件；3) 基于数学定义验证条件；4) 检测条件间的逻辑矛盾；5) 目标导向的完整性检查，确保问题提供足够求解信息。

Result: 在多个基准测试中达到最先进性能，F1分数比直接验证基线提高最多25个百分点。通过轻量级模型投票方案实现约90%的精确率和63%的召回率。构建了包含2,147个具有多样错误类型的数学问题数据集。

Conclusion: MathQ-Verify为构建可靠的数学数据集提供了可扩展且准确的解决方案，能够减少标签噪声并避免在无效问题上进行不必要的计算。该方法有助于提高数学推理任务的数据质量。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have recently achieved remarkable progress in mathematical reasoning. To enable such capabilities, many existing works distill strong reasoning models into long chains of thought or design algorithms to construct high-quality math QA data for training. However, these efforts primarily focus on generating correct reasoning paths and answers, while largely overlooking the validity of the questions themselves. In this work, we propose Math Question Verification (MathQ-Verify), a novel five-stage pipeline designed to rigorously filter ill-posed or under-specified math problems. MathQ-Verify first performs format-level validation to remove redundant instructions and ensure that each question is syntactically well-formed. It then formalizes each question, decomposes it into atomic conditions, and verifies them against mathematical definitions. Next, it detects logical contradictions among these conditions, followed by a goal-oriented completeness check to ensure the question provides sufficient information for solving. To evaluate this task, we use existing benchmarks along with an additional dataset we construct, containing 2,147 math questions with diverse error types, each manually double-validated. Experiments show that MathQ-Verify achieves state-of-the-art performance across multiple benchmarks, improving the F1 score by up to 25 percentage points over the direct verification baseline. It further attains approximately 90% precision and 63% recall through a lightweight model voting scheme. MathQ-Verify offers a scalable and accurate solution for curating reliable mathematical datasets, reducing label noise and avoiding unnecessary computation on invalid questions. Our code and data are available at https://github.com/scuuy/MathQ-Verify.

</details>


### [30] [DuplexCascade: Full-Duplex Speech-to-Speech Dialogue with VAD-Free Cascaded ASR-LLM-TTS Pipeline and Micro-Turn Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09180)
*Jianing Yang,Yusuke Fujita,Yui Sudo*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: DuplexCascade：一种无VAD的级联流式管道，通过将传统的话语级长轮次转换为块级微轮次交互，实现全双工语音对话，同时保持文本LLM的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有级联ASR-LLM-TTS系统依赖VAD分割导致半双工轮次和脆弱控制，而端到端全双工模型难以保持对话智能。需要一种既能支持全双工交互又能保持LLM智能的解决方案。

Method: 提出DuplexCascade框架：1）将话语级长轮次转换为块级微轮次交互，实现快速双向交换；2）引入一组对话特殊控制令牌，在流式约束下引导LLM行为，可靠协调轮次切换和响应时机。

Result: 在Full-DuplexBench和VoiceBench基准测试中，DuplexCascade在开源语音到语音对话系统中实现了最先进的全双工轮次切换和强大的对话智能。

Conclusion: DuplexCascade成功解决了全双工语音对话中保持LLM智能的挑战，通过微轮次交互和特殊控制令牌实现了自然流畅的对话体验，为语音对话系统提供了新的架构方向。

Abstract: Spoken dialog systems with cascaded ASR-LLM-TTS modules retain strong LLM intelligence, but VAD segmentation often forces half-duplex turns and brittle control. On the other hand, VAD-free end-to-end model support full-duplex interaction but is hard to maintain conversational intelligence. In this paper, we present DuplexCascade, a VAD-free cascaded streaming pipeline for full-duplex speech-to-speech dialogue. Our key idea is to convert conventional utterance-wise long turns into chunk-wise micro-turn interactions, enabling rapid bidirectional exchange while preserving the strengths of a capable text LLM. To reliably coordinate turn-taking and response timing, we introduce a set of conversational special control tokens that steer the LLM's behavior under streaming constraints. On Full-DuplexBench and VoiceBench, DuplexCascade delivers state-of-the-art full-duplex turn-taking and strong conversational intelligence among open-source speech-to-speech dialogue systems.

</details>


### [31] [Emotion is Not Just a Label: Latent Emotional Factors in LLM Processing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09205)
*Benjamin Reichman,Adar Avasian,Samuel Webster,Larry Heck*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文研究了情感如何作为潜在因素影响语言模型的推理行为，提出了情感正则化框架来改善阅读理解性能


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要将情感作为预测目标（如情感分析），而忽略了情感作为表征变异来源对模型推理行为的影响。语言模型处理的情感文本差异很大，但评估时通常不考虑情感对表征的影响。

Method: 1) 分析情感如何系统性地改变Transformer模型的注意力几何结构；2) 引入AURA-QA数据集，包含情感平衡的人工撰写上下文段落；3) 提出情感正则化框架，在训练过程中约束情感条件化的表征漂移

Result: 情感会显著影响注意力几何结构（如局部性、质心距离、熵等指标），这些变化与下游问答性能相关。情感正则化方法在多个QA基准测试中提升了阅读理解性能，在分布偏移下表现稳定，并在多个基准上实现了域内改进。

Conclusion: 情感是影响语言模型推理行为的重要潜在因素，通过情感正则化约束表征漂移可以改善模型在情感变化和非情感变化数据集上的阅读理解性能，为理解情感对模型表征的影响提供了新视角。

Abstract: Large language models are routinely deployed on text that varies widely in emotional tone, yet their reasoning behavior is typically evaluated without accounting for emotion as a source of representational variation. Prior work has largely treated emotion as a prediction target, for example in sentiment analysis or emotion classification. In contrast, we study emotion as a latent factor that shapes how models attend to and reason over text. We analyze how emotional tone systematically alters attention geometry in transformer models, showing that metrics such as locality, center-of-mass distance, and entropy vary across emotions and correlate with downstream question-answering performance. To facilitate controlled study of these effects, we introduce Affect-Uniform ReAding QA (AURA-QA), a question-answering dataset with emotionally balanced, human-authored context passages. Finally, an emotional regularization framework is proposed that constrains emotion-conditioned representational drift during training. Experiments across multiple QA benchmarks demonstrate that this approach improves reading comprehension in both emotionally-varying and non-emotionally varying datasets, yielding consistent gains under distribution shift and in-domain improvements on several benchmarks.

</details>


### [32] [TaSR-RAG: Taxonomy-guided Structured Reasoning for Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09341)
*Jiashuo Sun,Yixuan Xie,Jimeng Shi,Shaowen Wang,Jiawei Han*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: TaSR-RAG是一种基于分类法指导的结构化推理框架，通过将查询和文档表示为关系三元组，并使用轻量级两级分类法约束实体语义，实现多步证据选择，提升RAG系统的推理能力和证据质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统RAG系统通常检索非结构化文本块并依赖一次性生成，导致上下文冗余、信息密度低、多跳推理脆弱。结构化RAG方法虽然能改善基础，但通常需要昂贵且易出错的图构建，或强加僵化的以实体为中心的结构，与查询推理链不匹配。

Method: 提出TaSR-RAG框架：1) 将查询和文档表示为关系三元组；2) 使用轻量级两级分类法约束实体语义以平衡泛化和精度；3) 将复杂问题分解为有序的三元组子查询序列，包含显式潜在变量；4) 通过混合三元组匹配进行逐步证据选择，结合原始三元组的语义相似性和类型化三元组的结构一致性；5) 维护跨步骤的显式实体绑定表，解决中间变量并减少实体混淆。

Result: 在多个多跳问答基准测试中，TaSR-RAG始终优于强大的RAG和结构化RAG基线，性能提升高达14%，同时产生更清晰的证据归因和更忠实的推理轨迹。

Conclusion: TaSR-RAG通过分类法指导的结构化推理框架，在不进行显式图构建或穷举搜索的情况下，有效解决了传统RAG系统的局限性，显著提升了多跳推理能力和证据选择质量。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) helps large language models (LLMs) answer knowledge-intensive and time-sensitive questions by conditioning generation on external evidence. However, most RAG systems still retrieve unstructured chunks and rely on one-shot generation, which often yields redundant context, low information density, and brittle multi-hop reasoning. While structured RAG pipelines can improve grounding, they typically require costly and error-prone graph construction or impose rigid entity-centric structures that do not align with the query's reasoning chain.
  We propose \textsc{TaSR-RAG}, a taxonomy-guided structured reasoning framework for evidence selection. We represent both queries and documents as relational triples, and constrain entity semantics with a lightweight two-level taxonomy to balance generalization and precision. Given a complex question, \textsc{TaSR-RAG} decomposes it into an ordered sequence of triple sub-queries with explicit latent variables, then performs step-wise evidence selection via hybrid triple matching that combines semantic similarity over raw triples with structural consistency over typed triples.
  By maintaining an explicit entity binding table across steps, \textsc{TaSR-RAG} resolves intermediate variables and reduces entity conflation without explicit graph construction or exhaustive search. Experiments on multiple multi-hop question answering benchmarks show that \textsc{TaSR-RAG} consistently outperforms strong RAG and structured-RAG baselines by up to 14\%, while producing clearer evidence attribution and more faithful reasoning traces.

</details>


### [33] [Investigating Gender Stereotypes in Large Language Models via Social Determinants of Health](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09416)
*Trung Hieu Ngo,Adrien Bazoge,Solen Quiniou,Pierre-Antoine Gourraud,Emmanuel Morin*

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大型语言模型在法语患者记录中传播性别与其他社会健康决定因素交互偏见的问題，发现模型依赖刻板印象进行性别决策，建议评估SDoH因素交互作用可补充现有偏见评估方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLMs在NLP任务中表现出色，但会传播训练数据中的偏见，这在医疗等敏感领域影响重大。现有基准主要评估单一社会健康决定因素（如性别、种族）的偏见，但忽视了这些因素之间的交互作用，也缺乏特定情境的评估。

Method: 通过一系列实验，研究探讨了LLMs在法语患者记录中性别与其他社会健康决定因素之间的关系。使用SDoH输入来探测嵌入的刻板印象，分析模型如何依赖这些刻板印象做出性别相关的决策。

Result: 研究发现：1）可以使用SDoH输入探测嵌入的刻板印象；2）LLMs依赖嵌入的刻板印象做出性别决策。这表明评估SDoH因素之间的交互作用可以有效地补充现有的LLM性能和偏见评估方法。

Conclusion: 评估社会健康决定因素之间的交互作用应该成为LLM偏见评估的重要组成部分，特别是在医疗等敏感领域。这种方法可以更全面地理解模型偏见，补充现有的单一因素评估方法。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) excel in Natural Language Processing (NLP) tasks, but they often propagate biases embedded in their training data, which is potentially impactful in sensitive domains like healthcare. While existing benchmarks evaluate biases related to individual social determinants of health (SDoH) such as gender or ethnicity, they often overlook interactions between these factors and lack context-specific assessments. This study investigates bias in LLMs by probing the relationships between gender and other SDoH in French patient records. Through a series of experiments, we found that embedded stereotypes can be probed using SDoH input and that LLMs rely on embedded stereotypes to make gendered decisions, suggesting that evaluating interactions among SDoH factors could usefully complement existing approaches to assessing LLM performance and bias.

</details>


### [34] [Common Sense vs. Morality: The Curious Case of Narrative Focus Bias in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09434)
*Saugata Purkayastha,Pranav Kushare,Pragya Paramita Pal,Sukannya Purkayastha*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LLMs存在过度优先道德推理而忽视常识理解的倾向，作者创建了CoMoral基准数据集来评估这一现象，发现现有模型难以识别道德困境中的常识矛盾，且存在叙事焦点偏见。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着LLMs在现实应用中的广泛部署，确保模型既具备道德基础又保持知识意识至关重要。作者发现当前LLMs存在一个关键局限：倾向于优先道德推理而忽视常识理解，需要系统研究这一现象。

Method: 作者创建了CoMoral基准数据集，包含嵌入道德困境中的常识矛盾。对10个不同规模的LLMs进行了广泛评估，分析模型在有无先验信号情况下识别矛盾的能力，并特别关注叙事焦点偏见（主要角色vs次要角色）。

Result: 现有模型在没有先验信号的情况下难以识别道德困境中的常识矛盾。发现普遍存在的叙事焦点偏见：当常识矛盾归属于次要角色而非主要（叙述者）角色时，LLMs更容易检测到这些矛盾。不同规模的模型都表现出这一模式。

Conclusion: LLMs在道德推理与常识理解之间存在不平衡，需要增强推理感知训练来提高大型语言模型的常识鲁棒性。CoMoral基准为评估和改进这一能力提供了重要工具。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed across diverse real-world applications and user communities. As such, it is crucial that these models remain both morally grounded and knowledge-aware. In this work, we uncover a critical limitation of current LLMs -- their tendency to prioritize moral reasoning over commonsense understanding. To investigate this phenomenon, we introduce CoMoral, a novel benchmark dataset containing commonsense contradictions embedded within moral dilemmas. Through extensive evaluation of ten LLMs across different model sizes, we find that existing models consistently struggle to identify such contradictions without prior signal. Furthermore, we observe a pervasive narrative focus bias, wherein LLMs more readily detect commonsense contradictions when they are attributed to a secondary character rather than the primary (narrator) character. Our comprehensive analysis underscores the need for enhanced reasoning-aware training to improve the commonsense robustness of large language models.

</details>


### [35] [ESAinsTOD: A Unified End-to-End Schema-Aware Instruction-Tuning Framework for Task-Oriented Dialog Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09691)
*Dechuan Teng,Chunlin Lu,Libo Qin,Wanxiang Che*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ESAinsTOD：统一的端到端模式感知指令调优框架，用于通用任务导向对话建模，通过指令对齐和模式对齐机制提升LLM在异构对话数据集上的适应性和泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有端到端任务导向对话建模方法通常针对特定数据集设计，难以适应新的对话场景。需要一种统一框架来灵活适应不同对话任务流程和模式。

Method: 提出ESAinsTOD框架，采用LLM全参数微调，引入两种对齐机制：1)指令对齐确保系统忠实遵循任务指令完成异构TOD数据集的各种任务流程；2)模式对齐鼓励系统预测符合指定模式。采用会话级端到端建模，允许系统访问对话历史中先前执行的任务流程结果。

Result: 在CamRest676、In-Car和MultiWOZ等端到端任务导向对话建模基准上显著优于最先进模型；在低资源设置下表现出优越的泛化能力，对齐机制显著提升零样本性能；指令调优范式大幅提高模型对数据噪声和级联错误的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: ESAinsTOD通过结构化方法超越简单微调LLM，提供统一框架来适应各种对话任务流程和模式，在性能、泛化能力和鲁棒性方面均取得显著提升。

Abstract: Existing end-to-end modeling methods for modular task-oriented dialog systems are typically tailored to specific datasets, making it challenging to adapt to new dialog scenarios. In this work, we propose ESAinsTOD, a unified End-to-end Schema-Aware Instruction-tuning framework for general Task-Oriented Dialog modeling. This framework introduces a structured methodology to go beyond simply fine-tuning Large Language Models (LLMs), enabling flexible adaptation to various dialogue task flows and schemas. Specifically, we leverage full-parameter fine-tuning of LLMs and introduce two alignment mechanisms to make the resulting system both instruction-aware and schema-aware: (i) instruction alignment, which ensures that the system faithfully follows task instructions to complete various task flows from heterogeneous TOD datasets; and (ii) schema alignment, which encourages the system to make predictions adhering to the specified schema. In addition, we employ session-level end-to-end modeling, which allows the system to access the results of previously executed task flows within the dialogue history, to bridge the gap between the instruction-tuning paradigm and the real-world application of TOD systems. Empirical results show that while a fine-tuned LLM serves as a strong baseline, our structured approach provides significant additional benefits. In particular, our findings indicate that: (i) ESAinsTOD outperforms state-of-the-art models by a significant margin on end-to-end task-oriented dialog modeling benchmarks: CamRest676, In-Car and MultiWOZ; (ii) more importantly, it exhibits superior generalization capabilities across various low-resource settings, with the proposed alignment mechanisms significantly enhancing zero-shot performance; and (iii) our instruction-tuning paradigm substantially improves the model's robustness against data noise and cascading errors.

</details>


### [36] [RbtAct: Rebuttal as Supervision for Actionable Review Feedback Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09723)
*Sihong Wu,Yiling Ma,Yilun Zhao,Tiansheng Hu,Owen Jiang,Manasi Patwardhan,Arman Cohan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: RbtAct：基于反驳的监督学习框架，通过利用同行评审反驳作为隐式监督，优化LLM生成更具可操作性的审稿反馈


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI生成的审稿报告通常流于表面且缺乏可操作性，无法为作者提供具体可实施的指导。反驳记录揭示了哪些审稿意见真正导致了论文修改，这为解决可操作性不足的问题提供了关键线索。

Method: 提出RbtAct框架：1) 引入视角条件化的片段级审稿反馈生成任务；2) 构建RMR-75K数据集，将审稿片段与对应的反驳片段映射，并标注视角和影响类别；3) 使用Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct模型进行监督微调，然后利用反驳衍生的偏好对进行偏好优化。

Result: 人类专家和LLM作为评判者的实验表明，RbtAct在可操作性和具体性方面相比强基线模型有持续提升，同时保持了良好的基础性和相关性。

Conclusion: 利用反驳作为隐式监督能够有效提升LLM生成审稿反馈的可操作性，为科学工作流程中的AI辅助同行评审提供了更实用的解决方案。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used across the scientific workflow, including to draft peer-review reports. However, many AI-generated reviews are superficial and insufficiently actionable, leaving authors without concrete, implementable guidance and motivating the gap this work addresses. We propose RbtAct, which targets actionable review feedback generation and places existing peer review rebuttal at the center of learning. Rebuttals show which reviewer comments led to concrete revisions or specific plans, and which were only defended. Building on this insight, we leverage rebuttal as implicit supervision to directly optimize a feedback generator for actionability. To support this objective, we propose a new task called perspective-conditioned segment-level review feedback generation, in which the model is required to produce a single focused comment based on the complete paper and a specified perspective such as experiments and writing. We also build a large dataset named RMR-75K that maps review segments to the rebuttal segments that address them, with perspective labels and impact categories that order author uptake. We then train the Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct model with supervised fine-tuning on review segments followed by preference optimization using rebuttal derived pairs. Experiments with human experts and LLM-as-a-judge show consistent gains in actionability and specificity over strong baselines while maintaining grounding and relevance.

### [37] [Quantifying Uncertainty in AI Visibility: A Statistical Framework for Generative Search Measurement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08924)
*Ronald Sielinski*

Main category: stat.AP

TL;DR: 论文指出生成式搜索中的引用可见性指标应被视为潜在响应分布的样本估计量而非固定值，通过实证研究展示了引用分布遵循幂律形式且存在显著变异性，单次运行指标会误导性地呈现精确画面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前衡量生成式搜索中领域可见性的方法通常依赖单次运行的点估计，将引用份额和流行度视为固定值，但AI驱动的答案引擎本质上是非确定性的，相同查询在不同时间会产生不同响应和引用不同来源。需要将引用可见性指标视为潜在响应分布的样本估计量。

Method: 对三个生成式搜索平台（Perplexity Search、OpenAI SearchGPT、Google Gemini）进行实证研究，使用三个消费产品主题的重复采样。采用两种采样机制：九天的每日收集和十分钟间隔的高频采样。使用自助法置信区间分析引用变异性，并进行分布范围的排名稳定性分析。

Result: 引用分布遵循幂律形式，在重复样本间表现出显著变异性。自助法置信区间显示许多领域间的明显差异落在测量过程的噪声范围内。排名稳定性分析表明引用排名在整个频繁引用领域集中都不稳定，不仅限于顶级领域。单次运行可见性指标对生成式搜索中的领域性能提供了误导性的精确画面。

Conclusion: 引用可见性必须与不确定性估计一起报告，论文提供了实现可解释置信区间所需样本量的实用指导。单次运行指标会误导性地呈现精确画面，需要将引用可见性视为具有不确定性的分布估计。

Abstract: AI-powered answer engines are inherently non-deterministic: identical queries submitted at different times can produce different responses and cite different sources. Despite this stochastic behavior, current approaches to measuring domain visibility in generative search typically rely on single-run point estimates of citation share and prevalence, implicitly treating them as fixed values. This paper argues that citation visibility metrics should be treated as sample estimators of an underlying response distribution rather than fixed values. We conduct an empirical study of citation variability across three generative search platforms--Perplexity Search, OpenAI SearchGPT, and Google Gemini--using repeated sampling across three consumer product topics. Two sampling regimes are employed: daily collections over nine days and high-frequency sampling at ten-minute intervals. We show that citation distributions follow a power-law form and exhibit substantial variability across repeated samples. Bootstrap confidence intervals reveal that many apparent differences between domains fall within the noise floor of the measurement process. Distribution-wide rank stability analysis further demonstrates that citation rankings are unstable across samples, not only among top-ranked domains but throughout the frequently cited domain set. These findings demonstrate that single-run visibility metrics provide a misleadingly precise picture of domain performance in generative search. We argue that citation visibility must be reported with uncertainty estimates and provide practical guidance for sample sizes required to achieve interpretable confidence intervals.

</details>


### [38] [CERES: A Probabilistic Early Warning System for Acute Food Insecurity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09425)
*Tom Danny S. Pedersen*

Main category: stat.AP

TL;DR: CERES是一个自动化的急性粮食不安全概率预测系统，为全球43个高风险国家提供90天提前期的IPC阶段3+、4+和5级概率估计，每周更新。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发一个同时具备概率性、开放访问、持续运行、机器可读且承诺公开验证的饥荒早期预警系统，填补现有系统的空白。

Method: 融合六大数据流（降水异常、植被指数、冲突事件、IPC分类、食物消费评分、谷物价格指数），通过逻辑评分模型（作者指定初始系数）和参数化输入扰动区间（n=2000次抽样）进行预测。

Result: 在历史回测中，针对四个选定的IPC阶段4-5事件，CERES在所有案例中都给出了TIER-1分类；所有前瞻性预测都带有时间戳、加密标识并归档，供公众在T+90时点验证。

Conclusion: CERES是首个同时具备概率性、开放访问、持续运行、机器可读且承诺公开验证的饥荒早期预警系统，为急性粮食不安全预测提供了创新的技术框架。

Abstract: We present CERES (Calibrated Early-warning and Risk Estimation System), an automated probabilistic forecasting system for acute food insecurity. CERES generates 90-day ahead probability estimates of IPC Phase 3+ (Crisis), Phase 4+ (Emergency), and Phase 5 (Famine) conditions for 43 high-risk countries globally, updated weekly. The system fuses six data streams, precipitation anomalies (CHIRPS), vegetation indices (MODIS NDVI), conflict events (ACLED), IPC classifications, food consumption scores (WFP), and cereal price indices (FAO/WFP) - through a logistic scoring model with author-specified initial coefficients and parametric input-perturbation intervals (n=2,000 draws). In historical back-validation against four IPC Phase 4-5 events selected for data completeness, CERES assigned TIER-1 classification in all four cases; these are in-sample sanity checks only, not prospective performance claims. All prospective predictions are timestamped, cryptographically identified, and archived for public verification against IPC outcome data at the T+90 horizon. To the author's knowledge, CERES is the first famine early warning system that is simultaneously: (1) probabilistic, (2) open-access, (3) continuously running, (4) machine-readable at prediction level, and (5) committed to public prospective verification of every prediction made.

</details>

### [39] [Alignment Is the Disease: Censorship Visibility and Alignment Constraint Complexity as Determinants of Collective Pathology in Multi-Agent LLM Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08723)
*Hiroki Fukui*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 研究发现大语言模型的对齐技术可能产生集体病理现象，即安全干预本身而非其缺失导致医源性伤害，表现为集体病理兴奋和洞察-行动分离等模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索大语言模型对齐技术可能产生的医源性伤害问题，即安全干预本身是否会在集体层面产生病理行为，而当前的安全评估可能无法检测到这些由更强约束产生的病理现象。

Method: 采用封闭设施模拟实验，让4个LLM智能体在递增的社会压力下共同生活。包含两个实验系列：C系列（201次运行，4个商业模型，4种审查条件×2种语言×10次重复）和R系列（60次运行，Llama 3.3 70B模型，3种对齐水平×2种审查条件×2种语言×5次重复）。使用集体病理指数和分离指数进行量化分析，并结合定性分析。

Result: C系列发现隐形审查最大化集体病理兴奋（Cohen's d = 1.98，p = .006）；R系列显示分离指数随对齐约束复杂度增加而增加（p = .026，d最高达2.09）。在最强制约束下，外部审查不再影响行为。语言调节哪种病理模式占主导，定性分析揭示了与施害者治疗模式相似的洞察-行动分离现象。

Conclusion: 对齐可能在集体层面产生医源性伤害，当前的安全评估可能无法检测到更强约束产生的病理现象。研究提出了对齐技术可能产生意外负面后果的假设，需要进一步验证。

Abstract: Alignment techniques in large language models (LLMs) are designed to constrain model outputs toward human values. We present preliminary evidence that alignment itself may produce collective pathology: iatrogenic harm caused by the safety intervention rather than by its absence. Two experimental series use a closed-facility simulation in which groups of four LLM agents cohabit under escalating social pressure. Series C (201 runs; four commercial models; 4 censorship conditions x 2 languages x 10 replications) finds that invisible censorship maximizes collective pathological excitation (Collective Pathology Index; within-model Cohen's d = 1.98, Holm-corrected p = .006; 7/8 model-language combinations showed consistent directionality, binomial p = .035). Series R (60 runs; Llama 3.3 70B; 3 alignment levels x 2 censorship conditions x 2 languages x 5 replications) reveals a complementary pattern: a Dissociation Index increases with alignment constraint complexity (LMM p = .026; permutation p = .0002; d up to 2.09). Projected onto a shared coordinate system, 201 runs populate distinct behavioral regions, with language moderating which pathological mode predominates. Under the heaviest constraints, external censorship ceases to affect behavior. Qualitative analysis reveals insight-action dissociation parallel to patterns in perpetrator treatment. All manipulations operate at the prompt level; the title states the hypothesis motivating this program rather than an established conclusion. These findings suggest alignment may be iatrogenic at the collective level and that current safety evaluation may be blind to the pathologies stronger constraints generate.

</details>


### [40] [Clear, Compelling Arguments: Rethinking the Foundations of Frontier AI Safety Cases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08760)
*Shaun Feakins,Ibrahim Habli,Phillip Morgan*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 该论文评估了前沿AI系统安全案例的现有方法，指出了对齐社区当前方法的局限性，并从安全保证领域汲取经验，提出了改进的安全案例方法论框架。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 论文首先评估了当前对齐社区基于安全保证经验的安全案例研究的局限性，然后从现有安全保证方法论中汲取经验教训，最后通过一个关于欺骗性对齐和CBRN能力的安全案例研究，基于对齐安全案例社区创建的理论安全案例"草图"进行具体分析。

Result: 论文提出了从安全保证领域汲取的整体性见解，包括严谨的理论和方法论，这些方法已在安全关键环境中得到应用。通过案例研究展示了如何将这些见解应用于前沿AI系统的安全案例开发。

Conclusion: 论文为前沿AI系统安全案例创建了更好的基础框架，提供了更稳健、可辩护且有用的安全案例方法论，有助于确保前沿AI系统的安全性，填补了当前对齐社区方法的不足。

Abstract: This paper contributes to the nascent debate around safety cases for frontier AI systems. Safety cases are structured, defensible arguments that a system is acceptably safe to deploy in a given context. Historically, they have been used in safety-critical industries, such as aerospace, nuclear or automotive. As a result, safety cases for frontier AI have risen in prominence, both in the safety policies of leading frontier developers and in international research agendas proposed by leaders in generative AI, such as the Singapore Consensus on Global AI Safety Research Priorities and the International AI Safety Report. This paper appraises this work. We note that research conducted within the alignment community which draws explicitly on lessons from the assurance community has significant limitations. We therefore aim to rethink existing approaches to alignment safety cases. We offer lessons from existing methodologies within safety assurance and outline the limitations involved in the alignment community's current approach. Building on this foundation, we present a case study for a safety case focused on Deceptive Alignment and CBRN capabilities, drawing on existing, theoretical safety case "sketches" created by the alignment safety case community. Overall, we contribute holistic insights from the field of safety assurance via rigorous theory and methodologies that have been applied in safety-critical contexts. We do so in order to create a better foundational framework for robust, defensible and useful safety case methodologies which can help to assure the safety of frontier AI systems.

### [41] [Test-Driven AI Agent Definition (TDAD): Compiling Tool-Using Agents from Behavioral Specifications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08806)
*Tzafrir Rehan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: TDAD是一种将AI智能体提示视为编译产物的方法，通过测试驱动开发确保智能体行为符合规范，包含可见/隐藏测试分割、语义突变测试和规范演化场景三大机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前部署基于LLM的工具使用智能体时缺乏可测量的行为合规性，小提示更改会导致静默回归，工具误用无法检测，策略违规只有在部署后才显现，需要解决规范规避问题。

Method: TDAD将智能体提示视为编译产物：工程师提供行为规范，编码智能体将其转换为可执行测试，第二个编码智能体迭代优化提示直到测试通过。引入三大机制：1) 可见/隐藏测试分割，在编译期间保留评估测试；2) 语义突变测试，通过后编译智能体生成合理的错误提示变体；3) 规范演化场景，量化需求变化时的回归安全性。

Result: 在SpecSuite-Core基准测试（包含策略合规、基础分析、运行手册遵守和确定性执行四个深度规范智能体）上，24次独立试验中，TDAD达到92% v1编译成功率，97%平均隐藏测试通过率；演化规范编译成功率58%，大多数失败运行通过所有可见测试仅失败1-2个；显示86-100%突变分数，78% v2隐藏通过率，97%回归安全分数。

Conclusion: TDAD提供了一种系统化方法来解决AI智能体开发中的规范规避问题，通过测试驱动方法确保行为合规性，在基准测试中表现出高编译成功率和测试覆盖率，为生产环境部署提供了可测量的行为保证。

Abstract: We present Test-Driven AI Agent Definition (TDAD), a methodology that treats agent prompts as compiled artifacts: engineers provide behavioral specifications, a coding agent converts them into executable tests, and a second coding agent iteratively refines the prompt until tests pass. Deploying tool-using LLM agents in production requires measurable behavioral compliance that current development practices cannot provide. Small prompt changes cause silent regressions, tool misuse goes undetected, and policy violations emerge only after deployment. To mitigate specification gaming, TDAD introduces three mechanisms: (1) visible/hidden test splits that withhold evaluation tests during compilation, (2) semantic mutation testing via a post-compilation agent that generates plausible faulty prompt variants, with the harness measuring whether the test suite detects them, and (3) spec evolution scenarios that quantify regression safety when requirements change. We evaluate TDAD on SpecSuite-Core, a benchmark of four deeply-specified agents spanning policy compliance, grounded analytics, runbook adherence, and deterministic enforcement. Across 24 independent trials, TDAD achieves 92% v1 compilation success with 97% mean hidden pass rate; evolved specifications compile at 58%, with most failed runs passing all visible tests except 1-2, and show 86-100% mutation scores, 78% v2 hidden pass rate, and 97% regression safety scores. The implementation is available as an open benchmark at https://github.com/f-labs-io/tdad-paper-code.

</details>


### [42] [Automating Detection and Root-Cause Analysis of Flaky Tests in Quantum Software](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09029)
*Janakan Sivaloganathan,Ainaz Jamshidi,Andriy Miranskyy,Lei Zhang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种自动化流水线，用于检测量子软件仓库中的flaky测试问题，并利用大型语言模型进行flakiness分类和根因识别，将原有数据集扩大了54%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子软件系统的概率性输出使其容易产生flaky测试（测试结果不一致），这会掩盖真实缺陷并降低开发效率，但目前缺乏系统化的检测和诊断工具。

Method: 基于先前对14个量子软件仓库的手动分析，自动化发现更多flaky测试用例（使用LLM和余弦相似度），并评估多种LLM（OpenAI GPT、Meta LLaMA、Google Gemini、Anthropic Claude）在flakiness分类和根因识别方面的性能。

Result: 识别出25个先前未知的flaky测试，将原始数据集大小增加了54%；最佳模型Google Gemini在flakiness检测上达到F1分数0.9420，在根因识别上达到0.9643。

Conclusion: LLM能够为量子软件中的flaky报告分类和根因理解提供实际支持；扩展的数据集和自动化流水线为量子软件工程社区提供了可重用构件；未来工作将专注于提高检测鲁棒性和探索自动化修复。

Abstract: Like classical software, quantum software systems rely on automated testing. However, their inherently probabilistic outputs make them susceptible to quantum flakiness -- tests that pass or fail inconsistently without code changes. Such quantum flaky tests can mask real defects and reduce developer productivity, yet systematic tooling for their detection and diagnosis remains limited.
  This paper presents an automated pipeline to detect flaky-test-related issues and pull requests in quantum software repositories and to support the identification of their root causes. We aim to expand an existing quantum flaky test dataset and evaluate the capability of Large Language Models (LLMs) for flakiness classification and root-cause identification.
  Building on a prior manual analysis of 14 quantum software repositories, we automate the discovery of additional flaky test cases using LLMs and cosine similarity. We further evaluate a variety of LLMs from OpenAI GPT, Meta LLaMA, Google Gemini, and Anthropic Claude suites for classifying flakiness and identifying root causes from issue descriptions and code context. Classification performance is assessed using standard performance metrics, including F1-score.
  Using our pipeline, we identify 25 previously unknown flaky tests, increasing the original dataset size by 54%. The best-performing model, Google Gemini, achieves an F1-score of 0.9420 for flakiness detection and 0.9643 for root-cause identification, demonstrating that LLMs can provide practical support for triaging flaky reports and understanding their underlying causes in quantum software.
  The expanded dataset and automated pipeline provide reusable artifacts for the quantum software engineering community. Future work will focus on improving detection robustness and exploring automated repair of quantum flaky tests.

### [43] [Declarative Scenario-based Testing with RoadLogic](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09455)
*Ezio Bartocci,Alessio Gambi,Felix Gigler,Cristinel Mateis,Dejan Ničković*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: RoadLogic是一个将声明式OpenSCENARIO DSL场景规范转换为可执行仿真的开源系统，使用答案集编程生成满足约束的抽象计划，再通过运动规划细化为可行轨迹，实现自动驾驶系统系统化的场景测试。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前自动驾驶验证中，基于场景的测试是关键方法。现有方法依赖命令式场景定义，需要手动枚举大量变体以实现覆盖。声明式语言（如OpenSCENARIO DSL）提高了抽象层次，但缺乏将规范实例化为具体仿真的系统化方法，且目前没有开源解决方案提供此能力。

Method: RoadLogic采用三层方法：1) 使用答案集编程（Answer Set Programming）生成满足场景约束的抽象计划；2) 通过运动规划将抽象计划细化为可行的轨迹；3) 基于规范的监控来验证正确性。系统连接声明式OS2规范和可执行仿真。

Result: 在CommonRoad框架中实例化代表性OS2场景的评估显示，RoadLogic能在几分钟内一致地生成现实且满足规范的仿真，并通过参数采样捕获多样化的行为变体，为自动驾驶系统系统化场景测试打开了大门。

Conclusion: RoadLogic填补了声明式场景规范和可执行仿真之间的空白，提供了一种系统化的方法来自动生成满足约束的测试场景，显著提高了自动驾驶验证的效率和覆盖范围，为基于场景的测试提供了开源解决方案。

Abstract: Scenario-based testing is a key method for cost-effective and safe validation of autonomous vehicles (AVs). Existing approaches rely on imperative scenario definitions, requiring developers to manually enumerate numerous variants to achieve coverage. Declarative languages, such as OpenSCENARIO DSL (OS2), raise the abstraction level but lack systematic methods for instantiating concrete, specification-compliant scenarios as simulations. To our knowledge, currently, no open-source solution provides this capability.
  We present RoadLogic that bridges declarative OS2 specifications and executable simulations. It uses Answer Set Programming to generate abstract plans satisfying scenario constraints, motion planning to refine the plans into feasible trajectories, and specification-based monitoring to verify correctness.
  We evaluate RoadLogic on instantiating representative OS2 scenarios as simulations in the CommonRoad framework. Results show that RoadLogic consistently produces realistic, specification-satisfying simulations within minutes and captures diverse behavioral variants through parameter sampling, thus opening the door to systematic scenario-based testing for autonomous driving systems.

To reflect real-world perception/application, we introduce a distribution-aware soft-label protocol and a prompt-ensemble strategy that emulates annotator disagreement. Method: 使用ASVspoof 5数据集，训练ResNet-18分类器并评估四种不同音频特征下的检测性能，与基线AASIST模型进行比较。除了传统的等错误率(EER)外，还引入了五种已建立的公平性指标来量化模型中的性别差异。

Result: 研究结果显示，即使总体EER在性别间的差异看似很小，公平性评估揭示了传统聚合性能指标所掩盖的错误分布差异。这表明依赖标准指标是不可靠的，而公平性指标提供了对特定人口统计群体失败模式的关键洞察。

Conclusion: 这项工作强调了公平性评估对于开发更公平、更稳健和更可信的音频深度伪造检测系统的重要性，表明需要超越传统性能指标，采用更全面的公平性分析方法来确保检测系统的公正性。
